-->Carson<!-- -->.</span></p><ul class="answers"><li class="answer"><div class="answer-text" data-answer-id="0e730ecc-d5e6-357b-b801-2151eb2cab37" id="answer-id-0e730ecc-d5e6-357b-b801-2151eb2cab37" customer, (09.08.17)

Carson, 
The answer to your question is absolutely yes!. Although you are not a GamerClub member, you will still receive the collectible offerings! You have pre-ordered long in advance, but it does not count against you. To meet the final two requirement standards for the collectible offering you must :
(1) Pick up the game within 48 hrs (launch date: 10/27/17). (2) Satisfy the remaining balance owed.

*Note: 
Members of our BestBuy™ Gamers club'will receive nearly $12 off of every New Title that currently retails for $60 msrp. Also, your Gamer-points recieved will double when purchasing New games... Your account may very well recieve yet another $5-$10 voucher after earning the points. 

I hope my you found our answer helpful.
Thank you,
BestBuy™
